myrrour glaſſe chriſtes paſſion ❧ ❧ ❧ hh preface ¶to honorable lorde huſey lorde accordyngly vnto deſyre haue trāſlated boke put natyue mother tongue ſimple wit power lernyng wold ſuffer though nat ſo well done ſurely knowe many myght haue done wolde haue pleaſed lordſhip haue de • yred thē alſo wold haue lyked haue taken labour yet truſt haue ſo done may comforth reader hearer leſte haue gyuen occaſion ordre amend performe rudely barbarouſly ſet forward surely lorde chyefe cauſe labour thought boke ſhulde moche profytable reader edefyeng wolde diligently hear ſay treuth know thynge comfortable man amonges exercyſes helpe ſpirite obteyne loue god ſpecially hym yt wolde begyn vſe ſpiritual lyfe thynge thought always frutful thā continnal meditacion paſſion lorde god ieſus chriſt exercyſes ſpirituall meditacions may reduced brought vnto example man deſyre bewayll weape vice ſynnes vnkyndnes vilenes couit purge amend negligence defautes ſhall fynde none vehement redy meane pricke hym forwarde intent remembre moſt innocēt death paſſion redeamer conſyder bitter paynes ſuffred man ſpare kepe man payne eternall wherafter iuſtice ſhulde haue rather dampned man ſynnes man may ſee iuſtice alſo mercy god man may cōſyder hym ſelfe great mercy god god wold forgyue ꝑdon hym ſynnes may alſo perceiue iuſtice god owne ſynnes whiche god dyd correcte punyſſhe accordyng iuſtice hym ſelfe bycauſe wold nat ſuffre thē vnpuniſhed thus meditacion man may fynde weape mourne ſynnes ſon god bet woū dyd crucified god ſuffred cure man ſynnes kepe hym eternall payne may alſo man bewayle owne vnkyndnes conſyderyng vnkyndly rendreth ſo faythfull louer ſo many yuell dedes contrary goddes pleaſure alſo dayly contemptes deſpyſynges tendre loue kyndnes manyfolde gyftes man dayly receyueth hym morouer cōtemplacion death chriſt indureth man hope fear wherby may releaued two temptacyons • enormitie ſynnes moue man diſpaire hathe exerciſe wherby put away ſynnes make ſatisfactiō hath wherof redeme hīſelfe yt ye blode deth lorde god therfore nede nat feare ſynnes ſo ordre hym ſelfe yt dye chriſt dye ſay ſynne ryſe new lyfe parte man vexed preſumpcion vayne lyghtnes myrth without fear god hath abate vayne myrth cōſyderyng heuē ſhyt moſte holy frendes god many yeres ye aboue iiii thouſand yeres glory god denyed mā leaſt differred ſo many yeres vnto tyme lorde ſauiour ieſus whiche neuer dyd ſynne ſuffred death ſynne ſo mā may come glory payne thus ſhall mannes vayne myrth put downe peraduenture man dull ſlouthfull goodnes ſhall haue ſpedy remedy pricke forwarde dulnes cōſydre lorde god moſte pure innocent man ſuffred ſo greuouſe paynes hym man wold peraduenture exerciſe ſelfe owne knowlege ſo come meknes pray ſhall haue better occaſion therunto thā ponder way difformite great difference owne ſtudy labour ſhortly ordre hole lyfe labour lyfe ieſus chriſt remembre man howe cōtrarie thy lyfe wyl p̄ceptes vnlike vertues farre frō enſāples remēbre mā frayle thou art redy fal vnſtable thy good purpoſes vnredy rather loth folowe thy lorde howe vnapte goodnes euery man may dayly ſe hym ſelfe forthermore mā wold enflamed loue god may haue better help exerciſe natural rendre loue loue loue god neuer openly ſhewed man redemption paſſion death redeamer chriſt ieſus manifeſt remembraunce paſſion man moſte ſtrongly excited moued loue god man deſyre pricked forward loue let hym remembre benefites god ſignes token loue theſe benefites moſt euidently appere paſſion ye ſhall clerely ſe boke laſt man deſyre lyfe continuall perpetuall prayer wold haue herte euer lyfted vp god deuotion feruour euer renewed ſhal neuer get eaſly remembraunce lyfe paſſion lorde god may haue euery worde acte behauiour paine chriſt ſpake dyd vſed ſuffred compuncte ſory hert conforted ſpirite conſyderation may wepe compaſſion gyuyng thankes may haue ſwete affection nowe may deſyre confourmed vnto hym wyl may labour wyſſhe holly transfourmed hym thus may man go one helthe conforte ſoules nothyng harde vyle paynfull hym ſuffre god whiche dyd ſo great thynges hym ſo vyle wretche yea alſo thynketh thynges though neuer ſo paynefull ſwete pleaſaunt delectable commendable moche deſyred yf thereby may aſſimulate made lyke vnto mooſt ſhamefull paynefull dethe chriſte lorde god thoſe thynges faythfull ſeruant doeth gladly thoſe occupieth hym ſelfe aiudiouſly thoſe thynges ſercheth oft remembreth thoſe deſyreth fulfyll feruent mynde nat grudgynge ſayenge put vyle offyce ſhame labour payne rather thynkynge ſhal nat theſe thynges glad mynde doeth nat repute thynke hym ſelfe reputacion ſerueth god thynketh greate thynge wolde pleaſe almighty god onely goodnes accept vnto ſeruyce ſo vyle vnworthy mooſt myſerable wretche wherefore theſe thynges herte onely pleaſed may conformable lorde god doeth folow hym ſufferaunce trouble moche may hys frailtie ſuffreth knowledgeth ſynnes ioye lorde honoured glad pacience ſufferaunce tribulacions faythfull ſeruaunte hathe ſo ſtrongly ſubdued tyed appetyte vnder yocke captiuitie ryght reaſon ſhall nat haue wanton pleaſure carnall worldly deſyre yet vayne vnprofytable thynge alſo kepeth herte diligence caſtell greate ſtrengthe ſo wyll nat ſuffre ſynfull thought reſt therein yet vayne vnfruitfull imaginacions wandre therein euer thynkynge conſiderynge thoſe thynges ben ſpyrytuall godly inducyng vnto god great ioye deſyreth thoſe thinges feruently laboureth bryng effect moche lyfe euermore mooſt parte chaffe myxt corne therfore faythfull ſeruant taketh rydell wyndoſe diſcrecion hande ſo wyndeth purgeth chaffe corne doore herte taketh hande burnynge ſharpe ſwerde kepe diligently herte paradyſe god ſo ſo euer herte deſyreth eate tree lyfe ſuche thoughtes godlye ſpirituall lyuely ſuche though ſhe farre cuntrey yt place yet ſhe ſe holy aungels makynge great ioye bearynge ſoules thoſe holy martyr ſlayne battell vnto heuyn without purgatorye ſo bleſſyd woman ſeynge conceyued ſo feruent theſe thynges one theſe onys ye wold nat note queſtion mouyd good euyll perſons doth nat procede ignorance iuſte good perſons ſhal know ye werkes mercy done membres chriſte name loue reputeth thoſe good dedes done hym ſelfe alſo know ſhall haue great reward therby like maner euyll perſons ſhall knowe ſhalbe dampned contrary therfore aſked nat queſtion ignorāce queſtion great admiration meruell ye greatnes grace glorie whiche ſhalbe gyuen iuſte people thoſe good werkes alſo intollerable myſerie payne ſhall fall vpon euyll perſons theyr hardnes vnmercifulnesiaco 2 c ſo hard iudgement without mercy ſhalbe done hym wold ſhewe mercy ſhall deſerue ſteale rauiſhe mennys goodes ſythe eternally dampned wyll nat gyue theyr owne goodes almoſſe vnmerciful people ſhal ſuffre ſo greuouſe paynes ſhall ſuffre cruells • math omel 80 note criſoſtom ſayth payne euyll perſons euerlaſtyng ſo rewarde good men eternall ſynnes paſſe ye acte doyng yet remayneth gylt offence towardes god ſhalbe puniſhed good werkes loue god paſſe ſpeake acte dede yet remayne theyr merite ſo rewardyd god alſo ſaynt hierom ſayths • math 25 fine thou wyſe reader attende remēbre diligently paynes hell eternall alſo glorie heuyn life ſhall haue feare decay death therfore euangeliſt ſaythmath 25 euyll men ſhall go eternall fyre iuſte men euerlaſtynge life ioy heuyn prepared byfore begynnynge worlde therunto ware predeſtinate note wele predeſtination god nat neceſſarie cauſe thy ſaluation predeſtination god euer condicionally thyng predeſtinate vnder ſom cōdicion predeſtinate worlde ſhulde ſauid death ſon god watre baptiſme ſo wold receyue liue therafter alſo good iuſte men predeſtinate glorie eternall yet condicion contine true fayth charitie humilitie meknes pacience mercie pitie vertues operacion lord doth predeſtinate life euerlaſtyng ſeeth knoweth byfore ſhal haue ſuch vertues predeſtinacion myght ſay predeſtinate glorie ye haue ſuch vertues ye keape commaundimentes c ſo wyll nat keape goddes commaundymentes wyl nat continue fayth charitie good werkes c ſhall nat com end predeſtinacion glory heuyn wyl nat keape condicion therof therfore nat ouermoch attend truſt predeſtinacion god thou knowes nat rather attend wordes god thou heris knowis god true nat chaungeable ſo wordes true nat chaungedca 33 c let v thoſe wordes godca 18 e g prophet ezechiel ſayth perſon god nolo mortem impij ſed vt conuertatur via ſua et viuat si autem impius egerit poenitentiam ab omnibus peccatis ſuis et cuſtodierit omnia precepta mea vita viuet wyll nat ſayth almyghty god deth ſynner rather conuertyd ſyn liue grace ſynner penaunce ſory ſynnes hath keape preceptes true iudgement iuſtice ſhalliue grace ſhall nat dye eternally alſo ſaythmarci xvi qui crediderit et baptiſatus fuerit ſaluuus erit beleuith baptiſed ſo continueth true fayth promiſe made baptiſme ſhalbe ſaued alſo ſayth si vi ad vitam ingredi math 6 b ſerua mandata thou wylt cum lyfe euerlaſtyng keape commaundimentes place chriſt ſaythmath 19 c si dimiſeritis homnibus pecata eorum dimittet vobis pater meꝰ pecata veſtra ye forgyue men theyr offenſis heuenly father ſhall forgyue ſynnes theſe wordes many lyke ſtandeth predeſtinacion lyfe reprouyng death euer laſtyng loke none predeſtinacion thou keape theſe ſaynges god thou ſhalbe ſure therfore ſay nat many vnwyſe perſons ſay predeſtinate god ſauyd therfore nat dampned though neuer pray good deade aſſure thou keape nat commaūdimentes god c thou ſhalbe damned wherfore ware ſuch folyſhe ſaynges predeſtinacion god ſo ordred may obteyned goten prayer good laboures werkes hereunto ſaynt auſten ſayth thou nat predeſtinate labour thou may predeſtinate god ſeeth byfore man ſhalbe ſauyd ſo ſeeth ye meane maner ſhalbe ſauyd ſeeth ſhall ſake ſyn labour grace keape wyll god ſo ſauyd prayer lord ieſu chriſte iudge quicke deed vouchſafe order ſet laſt iudgement thy ryght hand may heare thy moſt ſwete voyce comforth thou ſhall ſpeake thy choſen people cum ye bleſſyd chylderne father take poſſeſſyon kyngdome glorie prepared byfore begynnyng worlde alſo keape feare nat hearynge moſte terrible ſentence thou ſhalt ſpeake vnto reprouyd ſynners ſaynge go ye curſed people euerlaſting fyer prepared dyuel compaygny thou onely begoten ſon god haue mercy v neuer fele incurable intollerable payne excludyd glory ſyght god burned perpetually euerlaſtyng fyre god mercy ſocour mercifull v amen ¶ thus endeth lytell treatyſe called glaſſe myrrour chriſtes paſſion imprynted london flete ſtrete ſygne george robert redman yere lorde god mcccccxxxiiii xii day
